208500000000     D*                                    part of the Create Table
208600000000     D*                                    statement.
208700000000     D*                                1 = Immediate. Data is inserted
208800000000     D*                                    initially.

260700000000     D*
260800000000     D*File Scope Array
260900000000     D*
261000000000     D*The file scope array is present for all Database files.
261100000000     D*The number of data members, Qdbflb#, contains the number of
261200000000     D*file scope array entries.  Each entry contains a based on
261300000000     D*physical file name, and optionally a record format name.
261400000000     D*
261500000000     D*Externally Described Physical Files:
261600000000     D*  There is only one entry.  The entry names the physical
261700000000     D*  file record format.  The file name portion of the entry
261800000000     D*  is NOT used.
261900000000     D*
262000000000     D*Program Described Physical Files:
262100000000     D*  There is one entry for each Data Dictionary record format.
262200000000     D*  The entry names the Data Dictionary record format.  The
262300000000     D*  file name portion of the entry is NOT used.
262400000000     D*
262500000000     D*Non-Join Logical Files:
262600000000     D*  There is one entry for each based on physical file.  Each
262700000000     D*  entry names the based on physical file and describes the
262800000000     D*  logical file record format to use with the based on file.
262900000000     D*
263000000000     D*Join Logical Files:
263100000000     D*  There is one entry for each based on physical file.  Each
263200000000     D*  entry names the based on physical file.  Only the first
263300000000     D*  entry describes the logical file record format to use with
263400000000     D*  the join logical file.
263500000000     D*
263600000000     D*SQL View Logical Files:
263700000000     D*  There is one entry for each based on physical file.  Each
263800000000     D*  entry names the base on file which will be either an
263900000000     D*  externally described physical file, or another view
264000000000     D*  logical file.  Only the first entry describes the logical
264100000000     D*  file record format to use with the view logical file.

276800000000     D****************************************************************
276900000000     D*
277000000000     D*Select/Omit Specification Array
277100000000     D*
277200000000     D*The Select/Omit specification array entries describe the
277300000000     D*record format's fields that the Select/Omit statements
277400000000     D*refer to.
277500000000     D*
277600000000     D*Non-Join Logical Files:
277700000000     D*  There can be one Select/Omit specification array for
277800000000     D*  each file scope array entry.
277900000000     D*
278000000000     D*Join Logical Files:
278100000000     D*  There can only be one Select/Omit specification array
278200000000     D*  for the join logical file.  The first scope array entry
278300000000     D*  for the join logical file will contain the offset to the
278400000000     D*  file's Select/Omit specification array.
278500000000     D*
278600000000     D*All Select/Omit specification arrays will end with an
278700000000     D*'AL' operation.
278800000000     D*
278900000000     D*Select/Omit constant operands have the following form:
279000000000     D*
279100000000     D*  Character   -  Quoted character string (imbedded quotes
279200000000     D*                 must be double quoted 'ISN''T').
279300000000     D*                 Blank padding will be done if the character
279400000000     D*                 constant passed is shorter than the field.
279500000000     D*
279600000000     D*  Hexadecimal -  X followed by a quoted string of valid
279700000000     D*                 hexadecimal values (X'F1F2F3').
279800000000     D*                 No padding will be done for a hexadecimal
279900000000     D*                 constant.  The length of a hexadecimal
280000000000     D*                 constant must exactly match the field
280100000000     D*                 length.
280200000000     D*
280300000000     D*  Floating    -  External form of floating point
280400000000     D*  Point          (1.234 E+10).
280500000000     D*
280600000000     D*  Packed or   -  String of 0 through 9 without decimal point.
280700000000     D*  Zoned or       The decimal point is assumed at the
280800000000     D*  Binary         appropriate precision.  The string must be
280900000000     D*                 Preceded by a - if negative and may be
281000000000     D*                 preceded by a + if positive (+1234 or
281100000000     D*                 -1234 would be +1.234 or -1.234 if the field
281200000000     D*                 was defined to have 3 decimal places).
281300000000     D*
281400000000     D****************************************************************
281500000000     D*This section can be located with the offset Qdbfsoof, which
281600000000     D*is located in the Scope array entry section.
281700000000     D****************************************************************
281800000000     DQDBQ37           DS
281900000000     D*                                Select/Omit Specification
282000000000     D*                                Array
282100000000     D QDBRSV54                1      2
282200000000     D*                                Reserved.

282600000000     D*                                      statement
282700000000     D*                                'O' = Select/Omit omit
282800000000     D*                                      statement
282900000000     D*                                'S' = Select/Omit select
283000000000     D*                                      statement

283400000000     D*                                'AL' = The Select/Omit
283500000000     D*                                       statement comparison
283600000000     D*                                       is for all (ALL)
283700000000     D*                                'EQ' = The Select/Omit
283800000000     D*                                       statement comparison
283900000000     D*                                       is for equal to
284000000000     D*                                       (COMP EQ).
284100000000     D*                                'GE' = The Select/Omit
284200000000     D*                                       statement comparison
284300000000     D*                                       is for greater than
284400000000     D*                                       or equal to (COMP GE).
284500000000     D*                                'GT' = The Select/Omit
284600000000     D*                                       statement comparison
284700000000     D*                                       is for greater than
284800000000     D*                                       (COMP GT).
284900000000     D*                                'LE' = The Select/Omit
285000000000     D*                                       statement comparison
285100000000     D*                                       is for less than or
285200000000     D*                                       equal to (COMP LE).
285300000000     D*                                'LT' = The Select/Omit
285400000000     D*                                       statement comparison
285500000000     D*                                       is for less than
285600000000     D*                                       (COMP LT).
285700000000     D*                                'NE' = The Select/Omit
285800000000     D*                                       statement comparison
285900000000     D*                                       is for NOT equal to
286000000000     D*                                       (COMP NE).
286100000000     D*                                'NG' = The Select/Omit
286200000000     D*                                       statement comparison
286300000000     D*                                       is for NOT greater
286400000000     D*                                       than (COMP NG).
286500000000     D*                                'NL' = The Select/Omit
286600000000     D*                                       statement comparison
286700000000     D*                                       is for NOT less than
286800000000     D*                                       (COMP NL).
286900000000     D*                                'VA' = The Select/Omit
287000000000     D*                                       statement comparison
287100000000     D*                                       is for values (VALUES)

412800000000     D*                                X'0001' = FLOAT  . . . . . .
412900000000     D*                                X'0002' = ZONED DECIMAL .  .

414400000000     D*                                X'8046' = DATALINK-OPEN  . .
414500000000     D*                                X'FFFF' = NULL . . . . . . .
414600000000     D*                                          NULL is only valid
414700000000     D*                                          for data base query
414800000000     D*                                          formats. If NULL is
414900000000     D*                                          specified, query
415000000000     D*                                          will determine the
415100000000     D*                                          type and attributes
415200000000     D*                                          of the field from

416000000000     D*                                (DF)              EXTRACT: Y
416100000000     D*                                (QQ)  QUERY:  R
416200000000     D QDBFFIOB               67     67
416300000000     D*                                Usage
416400000000     D*                                X'01' = Input-Only
416500000000     D*                                        The field can be used
416600000000     D*                                        for input operations
416700000000     D*                                        only.
416800000000     D*                                X'02' = Output Only
416900000000     D*                                        The field can be used
417000000000     D*                                        for output operations
417100000000     D*                                        only.
417200000000     D*                                X'03' = Both
417300000000     D*                                        The field can be used
417400000000     D*                                        for both input and
417500000000     D*                                        output operations.
417600000000     D*                                X'04' = Neither
417700000000     D*                                        The field can be used
417800000000     D*                                        for neither input nor
417900000000     D*                                        output operations.
418000000000     D*                                X'FF' = Unknown
418100000000     D*                                        The usage is set
418200000000     D*                                        appropriately during
418300000000     D*                                        query processing.

611900000000     D*
612000000000     D*         DERIVED FIELD DESCRIPTION INFORMATION
612100000000     D*
612200000000     D*The derived field structure is a stack of operators and
612300000000     D*operands in Reverse Polish Notation.  For example:
612400000000     D*
612500000000     D*   A + B would be:
612600000000     D*
612700000000     D*     A  B  +
612800000000     D*
612900000000     D*   ((A * B) + 14)/(X - Y) would be:
613000000000     D*
613100000000     D*     A  B  *  14  +  X  Y  -  /
613200000000     D*
613300000000     D*NOTE:  Numeric operands and character operands can not be
613400000000     D*mixed in one derived field description.  If numeric operands
613500000000     D*are specified, the resulting field attributes must be
613600000000     D*numeric.  If character operands are specified, the resulting
613700000000     D*field attributes must be character or DBCS.  Character and
613800000000     D*DBCS only fields cannot be mixed in one derived field
613900000000     D*description.
614000000000     D*
614100000000     D*Substringing DBCS fields will be allowed, although the data
614200000000     D*will be treated as character data, i.e. there is no true
614300000000     D*Double-Byte substring support.  This applies to query formats
614400000000     D*only.
614500000000     D*
614600000000     D*                                   (QQ)  QUERY:  Y
614700000000     D****************************************************************

614900000000     D*is located in the Field header section.

674800000000     D*     |                                             |
674900000000     D*     | Trigger attributes                          |
675000000000     D*     |   - TYPE - System or SQL                    |
675100000000     D*     |   - ORIENTATION - Column, Row, Statement    |
675200000000     D*     |   - TIME - Before/After                     |
675300000000     D*     |   - EVENT - Insert/Update/Delete/Read       |
675400000000     D*     |   - STATE - Enabled/Disabled                |
675500000000     D*     |                                             |
675600000000     D*     | Trigger program name and library            |
675700000000     D*     |                                             |
675800000000     D*     | Offsets to appended trigger areas for       |
675900000000     D*     |  this trigger definition. These offsets     |
676000000000     D*     |  are relative to the beginning of this      |
676100000000     D*     |  trigger definition header.                 |
676200000000     D*     |  - Trigger name area                        |
676300000000     D*     |  - SQL Path area                            |
676400000000     D*     |  - List of Update Columns                   |
676500000000     D*     |  - List of WHEN Referenced Columns          |
676600000000     D*     |  - List of BODY Referenced Columns          |
676700000000     D*     |  - List of Dependent Objects area           |
676800000000     D*     |  - Transition area                          |
676900000000     D*     |  - SQL Trigger STMT area                    |
677000000000     D*     |  - Trigger Text                             |
677100000000     D*     |                                             |
677200000000     D*     |  NOTE: A SYSTEM TRIGGER will have a         |
677300000000     D*     |        trigger header and a                 |
677400000000     D*     |        trigger name area. The text section  |
677500000000     D*     |        can only be added via the COMMENT    |
677600000000     D*     |        ON SQL statement and is therefore    |
677700000000     D*     |        optional. All other sections are     |
677800000000     D*     |        not applicable to a system trigger.  |
677900000000     D*     |                                             |
678000000000     D*     |        An SQL TRIGGER may have all of the   |
678100000000     D*     |        above structures with the following  |
678200000000     D*     |        restrictions/dependencies:           |
678300000000     D*     |        1 - The trigger definition header,   |
678400000000     D*     |            the trigger name area, the SQL   |
678500000000     D*     |            path, and the SQL trigger STMT   |
678600000000     D*     |            are all required.                |
678700000000     D*     |        2 - Only an SQL trigger with an      |
678800000000     D*     |            Update event will have a list of |
678900000000     D*     |            update columns.                  |
679000000000     D*     |        3 - The list of WHEN columns, the    |
679100000000     D*     |            list of BODY columns, the list   |
679200000000     D*     |            of dependent objects, and the    |
679300000000     D*     |            transition area are optional.    |
679400000000     D*     |            More correctly, they are         |
679500000000     D*     |            dependent on if there is any     |
679600000000     D*     |            of that type of information to   |
679700000000     D*     |            be included in the trigger       |
679800000000     D*     |            definition entry.                |
679900000000     D*     |        4 - The text section can only be     |
680000000000     D*     |            added via the COMMENT ON SQL     |
680100000000     D*     |            statement and is therefore       |
680200000000     D*     |            optional.                        |
680300000000     D*     |                                             |
680400000000     D*     |---------------------------------------------|
680500000000     D*     |                                             |
680600000000     D*     | TRIGGER NAME AREA - Fixed Length            |
680700000000     D*     |                                             |
680800000000     D*     | Length of the TRIGGER NAME AREA.            |
680900000000     D*     |   This length plus the offset to this       |
681000000000     D*     |   substructure will get addressability to   |
681100000000     D*     |   the next substructure in this trigger     |
681200000000     D*     |   definition.                               |
681300000000     D*     |                                             |

723300000000     D*                                             Qdb Qdbftrg Reserved11
723400000000     D*                                Reserved.                 @ADA

723600000000     D*                                             Qdb Qdbftrg Name Area Tot Le
723700000000     D*                                Total length of the trigger

724000000000     D*                                             Qdb Qdbftrg Name Lib Len

724500000000     D*                                Length of the trigger     @ADA
724600000000     D*                                name.
724700000000     D QDBQNS                 33     33
724800000000     D*                                             Qdb Qdbftrg Name Sysgen
724900000000     D*                                Trigger name generated by
725000000000     D*                                the system.
725100000000     D*                                X'00' => User GENed name.
725200000000     D*                                X'01' => Originally, user
725300000000     D*                                         GENed name but
725400000000     D*                                         collision occured
725500000000     D*                                         and system Re-GENed
725600000000     D*                                         the name.
725700000000     D*                                X'02' => System GENed name.
725800000000     D*                                                          @ADA

726000000000     D*                                             Qdb Qdbftrg Name Delim
726100000000     D*                                Trigger name is a delimited
726200000000     D*                                name. If a delimited name,
726300000000     D*                                then the name will contain
726400000000     D*                                double quotes.
726500000000     D*                                X'00' => Not delimited name.
726600000000     D*                                X'01' => Is a delimited name.
726700000000     D*                                                          @ADA

726900000000     D*                                             Qdb Qdbftrg Lib Delim
727000000000     D*                                Trigger library is a delimited
727100000000     D*                                name. If delimited,
727200000000     D*                                then the name will contain
727300000000     D*                                double quotes.
727400000000     D*                                X'00' => Not delimited name.
727500000000     D*                                X'01' => Is a delimited name.
727600000000     D*                                                          @ADA

727800000000     D*                                             Qdb Qdbftrg Name Type
727900000000     D*                                Trigger naming convention.
728000000000     D*                                X'00' => System naming.
728100000000     D*                                X'01' => SQL naming.      @ADA
728200000000     D QDBQR12                37     94
728300000000     D*                                             Qdb Qdbftrg Reserved12
728400000000     D*                                Reserved                  @ADA
728500000000     D QDBQNQ                 95    362
728600000000     D*                                             Qdb Qdbftrg Name Qual
728700000000     D*                                Qualified trigger name.
728800000000     D*                                The trigger name and library
728900000000     D*                                are in 2 parts.
729000000000     D*                                The first part contains the
729100000000     D*                                trigger library name (10
729200000000     D*                                characters).
729300000000     D*                                The second part contains the
729400000000     D*                                trigger name (258 characters).
729500000000     D*                                Qdb_Qdbftrg_Name_Len contains
729600000000     D*                                the length of the trigger
729700000000     D*                                name.
729800000000     D*
729900000000     D*                                The trigger name may be a
730000000000     D*                                delimited name (double
730100000000     D*                                quotes).
730200000000     D*                                Qdb_Qdbftrg_Name_Delim
730300000000     D*                                indicates whether it is
730400000000     D*                                delimited.  If it is
730500000000     D*                                delimited, the the name in
730600000000     D*                                this field does contain
730700000000     D*                                double quotes.
730800000000     D*
730900000000     D*                                The trigger library may be a
731000000000     D*                                delimited name (double
731100000000     D*                                quotes).
731200000000     D*                                Qdb_Qdbftrg_Lib_Delim
731300000000     D*                                indicates whether it is
731400000000     D*                                delimited.                @ADA

733900000000     D*
734000000000     D*List of Update Columns
734100000000     D*
734200000000     D*This is the list of columns specified for an Update trigger.
734300000000     D*The columns in this list must be present in the file's record
734400000000     D*format. The list will contain both the short and long column
734500000000     D*names.
734600000000     D*
734700000000     D*A seperate structure will be used to reference the column
734800000000     D*names since the long name can be variable length.
734900000000     D*
735000000000     D*NOTE: Each column entry name is unique. There will not be any
735100000000     D*   duplicate name entries.
735200000000     D*
735300000000     D*******************************************************************
735400000000     D*******************************************************************
735500000000     D*The following structure maps the UPDATE columns list entry
735600000000     D*******************************************************************
735700000000     DQDBFQULE         DS
735800000000     D*                                             Qdbf Qdbftrg Updc List Ent
735900000000     D QDBQULL                 1      4U 0
736000000000     D*                                             Qdb Qdbftrg Updc Le Len
736100000000     D*                                List Entry Length.
736200000000     D*                                Addressability to this entry
736300000000     D*                                plus this length gets
736400000000     D*                                addressability to the next
736500000000     D*                                column list entry.        @ADA
736600000000     D*
736700000000     D QDBQULSN                5     14
736800000000     D*                                             Qdb Qdbftrg Updc Le Short Na
736900000000     D*                                Short name of the column.
737000000000     D*                                                          @ADA

737200000000     D*                                             Qdb Qdbftrg Updc Le Short De
737300000000     D*                                Short name is delimited.
737400000000     D*                                X'00' => Name not delimited.
737500000000     D*                                X'01' => Name is delimited.
737600000000     D*                                                          @ADA
737700000000     D QDBQULLD               16     16
737800000000     D*                                             Qdb Qdbftrg Updc Le Long Del
737900000000     D*                                Long name is delimited.
738000000000     D*                                X'00' => Name not delimited.
738100000000     D*                                X'01' => Name is delimited.
738200000000     D*                                                          @ADA
738300000000     D QDBQULLS               17     17
738400000000     D*                                             Qdb Qdbftrg Updc Le Long Sam
738500000000     D*                                Short name and long name are
738600000000     D*                                the same.
738700000000     D*                                X'00' => Names are different.
738800000000     D*                                X'01' => Names are the same.
738900000000     D*                                                          @ADA
739000000000     D QDBQULLL               18     21U 0
739100000000     D*                                             Qdb Qdbftrg Updc Le Long Len
739200000000     D*                                Length of the long name -
739300000000     D*                                qdbfTRG_UPDC_LE_LONG_NAME
739400000000     D*                                                          @ADA

739600000000     D*                                             Qdb Qdbftrg Reserved17
739700000000     D*                                Reserved                  @ADA

739900000000     D*                                             Qdb Qdbftrg Updc Le Long Nam
740000000000     D*

740200000000     D*                                (varying length).
740300000000     D*                                                          @ADA

742900000000     D********************************************************************
743000000000     D*List of WHEN Reference Columns
743100000000     D*
743200000000     D*This is the list of the columns in the WHEN portion of the
743300000000     D*CREATE TRIGGER statement. Actually, the name is NOT part of the
743400000000     D*list. Rather, there is an offset to the column name in the WHEN
743500000000     D*statement of the expanded CREATE TRIGGER string.
743600000000     D*
743700000000     D*Each WHEN column entry consists of a set of offsets into the
743800000000     D*CREATE TRIGGER expanded string. The following is an example
743900000000     D*of the offsets.
744000000000     D*
744100000000     D*     Given Table T1 in LIB1 with columns COL1 and COL2
744200000000     D*     SQL will generate correlation variables X and Y.
744300000000     D*
744400000000     D*     If the user codes the following:
744500000000     D*
744600000000     D*     CREATE TRIGGER ...
744700000000     D*       AFTER INSERT ON T1 ...
744800000000     D*         WHEN(COL1 = COL2) ...
744900000000     D*
745000000000     D*     The expanded string will be in the form:
745100000000     D*
745200000000     D*     CREATE TRIGGER ...
745300000000     D*       AFTER INSERT ON LIB1.T1 X ...
745400000000     D*         WHEN(X.COL1 = X.COL2) ...
745500000000     D*
745600000000     D*     The correlation variable X is used to qualify the
745700000000     D*     column names with the library and file. The table in
745800000000     D*     the expanded string are qualified with the library
745900000000     D*     name.
746000000000     D*
746100000000     D*     The list entries will have offsets into the expanded
746200000000     D*     CREATE TRIGGER string.
746300000000     D*
746400000000     D*     ---------------------
746500000000     D*     | WHEN entry 1      |
746600000000     D*     | Offset to col ----|--------------+
746700000000     D*     | Offset to file ---|--------+     |
746800000000     D*+------| Offset to lib     |        |     |
746900000000     D*|      |-------------------|        |     |
747000000000     D*|      | WHEN entry 2      |        |     |
747100000000     D*|      | Offset to col ----|--------|-----|--------+
747200000000     D*|      | Offset to file ---|----+   |     |        |
747300000000     D*|   +--| Offset to lib     |    |   |     |        |
747400000000     D*|   |  ---------------------    |   |     |        |
747500000000     D*|   |                           |   |     |        |
747600000000     D*|   |                           |   |     |        |
747700000000     D*+-->+---------------+    +------+<--+     |        |
747800000000     D*                  |    |                |        |
747900000000     D*CREATE TRIGGER string V    V                V        V
748000000000     D*----------------------------------------------------------------
748100000000     D*| ... AFTER INSERT ON LIB1.T1 X ... WHEN(X.COL1 = X.COL2) ...  |
748200000000     D*----------------------------------------------------------------
748300000000     D*
748400000000     D*NOTE: The list of WHEN columns will identify all instances of a
748500000000     D*  column in the list. That is, there may be multiple
748600000000     D*  entries for the same column name. The first entry flag
748700000000     D*  can be used to differentiate between the first occurrence
748800000000     D*  of a column in the list and subsequent entries.
748900000000     D*
749000000000     D********************************************************************
749100000000     D*The following structure maps the WHEN columns array entry
749200000000     D********************************************************************
749300000000     DQDBQWA           DS
749400000000     D*                                             Qdb Qdbftrg When Array
749500000000     D QDBQWCO                 1      4U 0
749600000000     D*                                             Qdb Qdbftrg When Col Off
749700000000     D*                                WHEN column name offset into
749800000000     D*                                the WHEN portion of the CREATE
749900000000     D*                                TRIGGER statement.        @ADA
750000000000     D QDBQWCL                 5      8U 0
750100000000     D*                                             Qdb Qdbftrg When Col Len
750200000000     D*                                WHEN column name length.  @ADA
750300000000     D QDBQWFO                 9     12U 0
750400000000     D*                                             Qdb Qdbftrg When File Off
750500000000     D*                                Offset to the column's file
750600000000     D*                                name.                     @ADA
750700000000     D QDBQWFL                13     16U 0
750800000000     D*                                             Qdb Qdbftrg When File Len
750900000000     D*                                Length of the column's file
751000000000     D*                                name in the trigger string.
751100000000     D*                                                          @ADA
751200000000     D QDBQWLO                17     20U 0
751300000000     D*                                             Qdb Qdbftrg When Lib Off
751400000000     D*                                Offset to the column's file
751500000000     D*                                library name.             @ADA
751600000000     D QDBQWLL                21     24U 0
751700000000     D*                                             Qdb Qdbftrg When Lib Len
751800000000     D*                                Length of the column's file
751900000000     D*                                library name.             @ADA
752000000000     D QDBQW1E                25     25
752100000000     D*                                             Qdb Qdbftrg When 1st Entry
752200000000     D*                                Indicates if the column name
752300000000     D*                                is the first in the list of
752400000000     D*                                entries.
752500000000     D*                                X'00' => Column is 2nd or
752600000000     D*                                         greater occurance
752700000000     D*                                         in the list.
752800000000     D*                                X'01' => Column is the first
752900000000     D*                                         in the list.     @ADA
753000000000     D QDBQWTF                26     26
753100000000     D*                                             Qdb Qdbftrg When This File
753200000000     D*                                Indicates if the column name
753300000000     D*                                is in this FILE. That is,
753400000000     D*                                the column name is in the
753500000000     D*                                same file as the trigger.
753600000000     D*                                X'00' => Column not in THIS
753700000000     D*                                         FILE.
753800000000     D*                                X'01' => Column in THIS FILE.
753900000000     D*                                                          @ADA
754000000000     D QDBQWCL00              27     27
754100000000     D*                                             Qdb Qdbftrg When Col Long
754200000000     D*                                Indicates if the column name
754300000000     D*                                is a short or long name.
754400000000     D*                                X'00' => Name is short name.
754500000000     D*                                X'01' => Name is long name.
754600000000     D*                                                          @ADA
754700000000     D QDBQWCD                28     28
754800000000     D*                                             Qdb Qdbftrg When Col Del
754900000000     D*                                Indicates if the column name
755000000000     D*                                is a delimited name.
755100000000     D*                                X'00' => Name non-delimited.
755200000000     D*                                X'01' => Name is delimited.
755300000000     D*                                                          @ADA
755400000000     D QDBQWFL00              29     29
755500000000     D*                                             Qdb Qdbftrg When File Long
755600000000     D*                                Indicates if the column's FILE
755700000000     D*                                name is a short or long name.
755800000000     D*                                X'00' => Name is short name.
755900000000     D*                                X'01' => Name is long name.
756000000000     D*                                                          @ADA
756100000000     D QDBQWFD                30     30
756200000000     D*                                             Qdb Qdbftrg When File Del
756300000000     D*                                Indicates if the column's
756400000000     D*                                FILE name is a delimited name.
756500000000     D*                                X'00' => Name non-delimited.
756600000000     D*                                X'01' => Name is delimited.
756700000000     D*                                                          @ADA
756800000000     D QDBQWLL00              31     31
756900000000     D*                                             Qdb Qdbftrg When Lib Long
757000000000     D*                                Indicates if the column's LIB
757100000000     D*                                name is a short or long name.
757200000000     D*                                X'00' => Name is short name.
757300000000     D*                                X'01' => Name is long name.
757400000000     D*                                                          @ADA
757500000000     D QDBQWLD                32     32
757600000000     D*                                             Qdb Qdbftrg When Lib Del
757700000000     D*                                Indicates if the column's
757800000000     D*                                LIB name is a delimited name.
757900000000     D*                                X'00' => Name non-delimited.
758000000000     D*                                X'01' => Name is delimited.
758100000000     D*                                                          @ADA
758200000000     D QDBQR20                33     64
758300000000     D*                                             Qdb Qdbftrg Reserved20
758400000000     D*                                Reserved                  @ADA
758500000000     D********************************************************************
758600000000     D*The following structure maps the WHEN columns structure
758700000000     D********************************************************************
758800000000     DQDBQWA00         DS
758900000000     D*                                             Qdb Qdbftrg When Area
759000000000     D QDBQR18                 1     20
759100000000     D*                                             Qdb Qdbftrg Reserved18
759200000000     D*                                Reserved.                 @ADA
759300000000     D QDBQWTL                21     24U 0
759400000000     D*                                             Qdb Qdbftrg When Tot Len
759500000000     D*                                Length of the WHEN
759600000000     D*                                referenced columns area.  @ADA
759700000000     D QDBQWNC                25     28U 0
759800000000     D*                                             Qdb Qdbftrg When Num Cols
759900000000     D*                                Number of columns in the list.
760000000000     D*                                                          @ADA
760100000000     D QDBQWSR                29     29
760200000000     D*                                             Qdb Qdbftrg When Self Ref
760300000000     D*                                Indicates columns in the
760400000000     D*                                WHEN list belong to this file.
760500000000     D*                                That is, this is a self-
760600000000     D*                                referencing dependency.
760700000000     D*                                X'00' => All self-referencing.
760800000000     D*                                         All columns belong
760900000000     D*                                         to the ON table.
761000000000     D*                                X'01' => Self-referencing.
761100000000     D*                                         Some of the columns
761200000000     D*                                         belong to the ON
761300000000     D*                                         table.
761400000000     D*                                X'02' => Not self-referencing.
761500000000     D*                                         None of the columns
761600000000     D*                                         belong to the ON
761700000000     D*                                         table.
761800000000     D*
761900000000     D QDBQR19                30     80
762000000000     D*                                             Qdb Qdbftrg Reserved19
762100000000     D*                                Reserved                  @ADA
762200000000     D*QDBQWA01                      64

765500000000     D********************************************************************
765600000000     D*The following structure maps the BODY columns structure
765700000000     D*
765800000000     D*List of Columns referenced in the BODY
765900000000     D*
766000000000     D*This is the list of the columns in the BODY portion of the
766100000000     D*CREATE TRIGGER statement.
766200000000     D*
766300000000     D*The columns in this list may be in this file or another file.
766400000000     D*
766500000000     D*NOTE: This is not the actual list but a set of offsets into the
766600000000     D*  SQL CREATE TRIGGER stmt that will position one to a
766700000000     D*  column name in the BODY.
766800000000     D*
766900000000     D*  See the WHEN columns prologue for an example of how
767000000000     D*  column entry offsets are tied to the CREATE TRIGGER string.
767100000000     D*
767200000000     D*NOTE: The list of BODY columns will identify all instances of a
767300000000     D*  column in the list. That is, there may be multiple
767400000000     D*  entries for the same column name. The first entry flag
767500000000     D*  can be used to differentiate between the first occurrence
767600000000     D*  of a column in the list and subsequent entries.
767700000000     D*
767800000000     D********************************************************************
767900000000     D*The following structure maps the BODY column array entry
768000000000     D********************************************************************
768100000000     DQDBQBA00         DS
768200000000     D*                                             Qdb Qdbftrg Body Array
768300000000     D*                                Individual BODY Column Entry.
768400000000     D*                                Note: This structure does
768500000000     D*                                not contain the name of a
768600000000     D*                                column in the trigger body,
768700000000     D*                                but an offest into the
768800000000     D*                                trigger body where the
768900000000     D*                                column is referenced.
769000000000     D*                                Each entry is 64 bytes long.
769100000000     D*                                                          @ADA
769200000000     D QDBQBCO                 1      4U 0
769300000000     D*                                             Qdb Qdbftrg Body Col Off
769400000000     D*                                BODY Column Name offset into
769500000000     D*                                the BODY portion of the
769600000000     D*                                CREATE TRIGGER statement. @ADA
769700000000     D QDBQBCL                 5      8U 0
769800000000     D*                                             Qdb Qdbftrg Body Col Len
769900000000     D*                                Length of the column name in
770000000000     D*                                the trigger string.       @ADA
770100000000     D QDBQBFO                 9     12U 0
770200000000     D*                                             Qdb Qdbftrg Body File Off
770300000000     D*                                Offset to the column's file
770400000000     D*                                name.                     @ADA
770500000000     D QDBQBFL                13     16U 0
770600000000     D*                                             Qdb Qdbftrg Body File Len
770700000000     D*                                Length of the column's file
770800000000     D*                                name in the trigger string.
770900000000     D*                                                          @ADA
771000000000     D QDBQBLO                17     20U 0
771100000000     D*                                             Qdb Qdbftrg Body Lib Off
771200000000     D*                                Offset to the column's library
771300000000     D*                                name.                     @ADA
771400000000     D QDBQBLL                21     24U 0
771500000000     D*                                             Qdb Qdbftrg Body Lib Len
771600000000     D*                                Length of the column's library
771700000000     D*                                name in the trigger string.
771800000000     D*                                                          @ADA
771900000000     D QDBQB1E                25     25
772000000000     D*                                             Qdb Qdbftrg Body 1st Entry
772100000000     D*                                Indicates if the column name
772200000000     D*                                is the first in the list of
772300000000     D*                                entries.
772400000000     D*                                X'00' => Column is 2nd or
772500000000     D*                                         greater occurance
772600000000     D*                                         in the list.
772700000000     D*                                X'01' => Column is the first
772800000000     D*                                         in the list.     @ADA
772900000000     D QDBQBTF                26     26
773000000000     D*                                             Qdb Qdbftrg Body This File
773100000000     D*                                Indicates if the column name
773200000000     D*                                is in this FILE. That is,
773300000000     D*                                the column name is in the
773400000000     D*                                same file as the trigger.

773600000000     D*                                         FILE.

785100000000     D*
785200000000     D*List of Dependent Objects for the WHEN/BODY clauses.

785400000000     D*NOTE: This is not the actual list but a set of offsets into the

785600000000     D*   dependent object.

786300000000     D*   of an object in the list. That is, there may be multiple

815400000000     D*******************************************************************
815500000000     D*
815600000000     D*SQL TRIGGER STMT AREA
815700000000     D*
815800000000     D*NOTE: This is the complete CREATE TRIGGER statement and expanded
815900000000     D*   to include library information.
816000000000     D*
816100000000     D*NOTE: All offsets are relative to the beginning of the CREATE
816200000000     D*   TRIGGER string.
816300000000     D*
816400000000     D*DESIGN NOTE: The expanded string for the CREATE TRIGGER will be
816500000000     D*    library qualified for both SQL names and system names.
816600000000     D*    That is, for those object names not library qualified,
816700000000     D*    one will be added before the object name. All names
816800000000     D*    (short, long, delimited, non-delimited) will be left as
816900000000     D*    the user specified them.
817000000000     D*
817100000000     D*    The design point will be to store the image of what the
817200000000     D*    user defined but with all names library qualified.
817300000000     D*
817400000000     D*    For column names, correlation variables will be used
817500000000     D*    for each column to qualify the names.
817600000000     D*
817700000000     D*    For example:
817800000000     D*
817900000000     D*      Given Table T1 in LIB1 with columns COL1 and COL2
818000000000     D*      Given Table T2 in LIB2 with columns COL3 and COL4
818100000000     D*      SQL will generate correlation variables X and Y
818200000000     D*
818300000000     D*      If the user codes the following:
818400000000     D*
818500000000     D*      CREATE TRIGGER ... SELECT * FROM T1, T2 WHEN COL1 = 10
818600000000     D*
818700000000     D*      The expanded string will be in the form:
818800000000     D*
818900000000     D*      CREATE TRIGGER ...
819000000000     D*        SELECT X.COL1, X.COL2, Y.COL3, Y.COL4
819100000000     D*          FROM LIB1.T1 X, LIB2.T2 Y
819200000000     D*            WHEN X.COL1 = 10
819300000000     D*
819400000000     D*      The correlation variables X and Y are used to qualify
819500000000     D*      the column names with the library and file. The tables
819600000000     D*      in the expanded string are qualified with the library
819700000000     D*      name.
819800000000     D*
819900000000     D*******************************************************************
820000000000     DQDBQSA           DS
820100000000     D*                                             Qdb Qdbftrg Stmt Area
820200000000     D*                                SQL Trigger statement area.
820300000000     D*                                                          @ADA
820400000000     D QDBQR29                 1     20
820500000000     D*                                             Qdb Qdbftrg Reserved29
820600000000     D*                                Reserved.                 @ADA
820700000000     D QDBQSTL                21     24U 0
820800000000     D*                                             Qdb Qdbftrg Stmt Tot Len
820900000000     D*                                Total length of the SQL
821000000000     D*                                Trigger statement area -
821100000000     D*                                substructure
821200000000     D*                                Qdb_Qdbftrg_Stmt_Area.    @ADA
821300000000     D QDBQSOO                25     28U 0
821400000000     D*                                             Qdb Qdbftrg Stmt Onfile Off
821500000000     D*                                Offset to the user specified
821600000000     D*                                file/table name in the
821700000000     D*                                CREATE TRIGGER STMT.
821800000000     D*                                This is the ON table-name
821900000000     D*                                that specifies the table
822000000000     D*                                the trigger is being added
822100000000     D*                                to. See the prologue of this
822200000000     D*                                structure for the layout of
822300000000     D*                                the data.                 @ADA
822400000000     D*
